2) New:         Added function cat_vol_maskimage for lesion masking to 
                avoid deformation in these areas.

                between registration with(out) manual lesion data.
                Added handling for output of lesion maps.

                regions that sometimes strongly increased processing time
                (thanks to Gabriel Ziegler for pointing out that issue).

                cat_vol_partvol by detecting large untypical CSF areas
                (and strongly (asymmetric) deformed regions), followed by
                a region-growing. The detection of asymmetric regions is 
                defined in cat_main but is inactive because it works only 
                in single cases yet.

r1325 | dahnke | 2018-06-20 19:57:53 +0200 (Mi, 20 Jun 2018) | 48 lines

Changed paths:
M       CHANGES.txt
M       cat_conf_extopts.m
M       cat_conf_tools.m
M       cat_defaults.m
M       cat_io_colormaps.m
M       cat_main.m
M       cat_main_registration.m
M       cat_run_job.m
M       cat_run_job1070.m
M       cat_surf_render2.m
M       cat_vol_partvol.m
M       ds.m
M       tbx_cfg_cat.m

PART A - WMHs: 
1) Changed:     Removed WMHCstr parameter from expert GUI to focus on the 
                standard case (changed to 0.5 in cat_defaults). 
2) Changed:     Moved WMHC correction after AMAP processing (cat_main). 
                WMH regions were now handled as GM in the initial AMAP 
                segmentation. After AMAP all GM voxels in WMH regions were
                set as GM (WMHC<2), WM (WMHC=2) or as extra class (WMHC=3).
                Added warnings in case of bad combinations of WMHC and
                WMHCstr that use no correction but output images.            
3) Changed:     The WMHs required an updated of the internal scaling of
                Yp0b in cat_main from 3 to 5 classes to have round uint8 
                values of a tissue class, ie. with a WM value of 255/5*3.                 

PART B - Lesion handling controlled by WMHC: 
1) New:         Added further cases to the WMHC parameter to handle the 
                lesion processing (WMHC=4). Added a simple detection of 
                very large lesion in cat_vol_partvol (WMHC=5).
2) New:         Added lesion handling by zero values in the original
                dataset that were now ignored in the Dartel/Shooting
                deformation process (cat_main_registration).               
3) New:         Because of the internal interpolation the detection of
                manual lesions (zero values in the brain) is located in 
                the cat_run_job(1070). 
4) New:         Added batch for lesion and brain masking (cat_conf_tools). 
                
PART C - Other changes: 
1) Changed:     Removed some gcutstr expert options because of to many 
                options and to unspecific/small/useless changes. 
2) Changed:     Small cleanup and modifications in cat_io_colormaps. 
3) Fixed:       Corrected small bug in cat_surf_render2.

r1248 | gaser | 2017-12-15 13:06:59 +0100 (Fr, 15 Dez 2017) | 27 lines

Changed paths:
M       CAT12-Manual.docx
M       CAT12-Manual.pdf
M       CHANGES.txt
M       Contents.m
M       cat_conf_stools.m
M       cat_surf_resamp.m
M       cat_surf_resamp_freesurfer.m
M       check_pipeline/batch_surface_pipeline.m
M       html/cat.html
M       html/cat_starting.html

(1) Fixed: Heat kernel smoothing was resolution dependent. Solved that issue
    and additionally replaced the weighting for filtering meshes with equal 
    weighting. Sigma is now the mean point distance. For cortical thickness 
    a good starting value is now 12-15mm, while other surface parameters 
    based on cortex folding (e.g. gyrification, cortical complexity) need a 
    larger filter size of about 20-25mm. Please update your scripts 
    and replace the old field "fwhm" by "fwhm_surf" and adapt the values.
(1) Changed: Again added option for 32k meshes because smoothing size
    is not correct for these meshes.
(2) Changed: Added warning if old scripts with "fwhm" filed are used in 
    cat_surf_resamp.m.
(3) Changed: The new name for resampled and smoothed surface data is not 
    containing "mm" anymore to indicate the filter size. This is also thought 
    to not mix data smoothed with the old and new smoothing method.

(1) Changed: Added remsampling to 32k mesh from Human Connectome Project
    (HCP). This allows faster and less memory demanding processing and 
    provides compatibility to the HCP. Another advantage is that left and 
    right hemispheres are aligned to optionally allow a direct comparison
    between hemispheres.
(2) Changed: Made all necessary functions compatible to 32k meshes.
(3) Added: New folders templates_surfaces_32k and atlases_surfaces_32k
(4) Fixed: Camlight and axes issue in cat_surf_results.m
(5) Changed: Renamed some files in templates_surfaces.

r1153 | dahnke | 2017-07-05 17:40:07 +0200 (Mi, 05 Jul 2017) | 23 lines

Changed paths:
M       CHANGES.txt
M       templates_1.50mm/Template_0_IXI555_MNI152_GS.nii
M       templates_1.50mm/Template_1_IXI555_MNI152_GS.nii
M       templates_1.50mm/Template_2_IXI555_MNI152_GS.nii
M       templates_1.50mm/Template_3_IXI555_MNI152_GS.nii
M       templates_1.50mm/Template_4_IXI555_MNI152_GS.nii

Changed:  Updated the Shooting template by a 1.5 mm version of the IXI template 
          processed with 1.0 mm and modified Shooting parameter with reduced 
          decay of coarse to fine schedule 
              lam = 1/3;  % default 0.5
          and adapted schedule parameter 
              d.sched = (d.sched - d.sched(end)) / diff([d.sched(end), ...
                         d.sched(1)])*(inter-1)+1;
          rather than
              d.sched = d.sched/d.sched(end);
          to a similar spectrum of values with smoother changes to increase the 
          amount of low frequency deformation and have smooth changes at all
          template stages. Keep in mind that even this template show much more
          anatomical details than the Dartel template, it requires less strong
          deformations to achieve this!

                 registration in cat_run_job. For initial affine registration a 
                 brain mask is applied to the template. Furthermore, the number 
                 of gaussian classes is corrected and checkt after the first 
                 SPM preprocessing.

                 of the image, than the COM is used to reinitialise the the
                 registration (cat_run_job).

                 cat_run_job.                
(4)  Changed:    Refined the fine affine registration in cat_run_job by further 
                 steps to reduce problems in R1 weighted scans and skull-striped
                 data. In case of skull-stripped data the brain mask is used. 
(4)  Changed:    Added cat_spm_affreg to avoid popup error message in case of 
                 initial affine registration errors that are maybe fixed by 
                 COM initialisation or spm_maff8. 
(5)  Changed:    Removed affreg case 'subj' regularisation because the results  
                 were equivalent with the case 'none' registration.  
                 Added comments for some parameter in cat_conf_opts. 
(6)  Fixed:      Corrected problems in cat_main_gintnorm and cat_main_LAS for  
                 inverse contrasts.

A       html/images/cat_tst_seg_sve_boxplot.png
A       html/images/neonates.png
M       html/style.css
M       internal/cat_vol_flipside.m

== New ==
(1) New*:      Added processing of images with BG<GM<WM<CSF contrast (neonates)
               as separate case that does not influence the default pipeline.
(2) New:       Added further preliminary validation results figures that are not
               linked in the help. 
   
== Parameterupdates ==              
(1) Changed:   opt.ngauss: 
               Updated SPM ngauss parameter in cat_defaults with only one      
               rather than three GM and WM classes because it was more stable   
               onthe BWP and real Datasets.  More than one GM and WM gaussian   
               peaks seams to bet better in case of inverse data (T2/PD). 
               Hence, an automatically switch to more than three GM and WM 
               peaks is added in the cat_run_job. 
(2) Changed:   extopts.resval & extopts.restype: 
               Increased the upper limit of the internal interpolation to 0.5 mm  
               rather than 1.0 mm (resval = [0.5 0.3]) and add 1.0 mm as minimum
               resolution to improve the results in case of anisotropic high- 
               resolution data (e.g., 0.5x0.5x1.5 mm) but also of low resolution
               data of the default interpolation option (restype = 'best'). 
(3) Changed:   opt.biasreg, opt.biasfwhm & opt.biasstr:
               Added opts.biasstr parameter to the cat_default-file and to  
               the GUI to have a simple control parameter for inhomogeneity 
               correction that controls the SPM preprocessing parameter 
               opts.biasreg and opts.biasfwhm that were removed at once 
               from the expert GUI. 
(4) Changed:   Corrected LASstr parameter to give optimal results for 0.5.               
(5) Changed:   opts.warpreg:
               Removed opts.warpreg parameter from expert GUI because our test
               indicated no useful changes with no general effects and only
               worse results in single cases.
(6) Changed:   Added additional sub parameter for lab operation in cat_vol_morph
               to allow more than one large cluster.
       
               
== Other Updates ==              
(1) Changed:   Replace old SPM tissue threshold estimation by the @-function 
               "clsint" in cat_main, cat_main_gintnorm.  
(2) Changed:   Added transparency and saturation parameter to cat_plot_boxplot. 
(3) Changed:   Forced low change rate for first Shooting template to improve 
               Shooting quality of lower regstr values.
(4) Changed:   Added resolution dependency for cleanup of the initial SPM 
               segmentation to avoid problems in case of low resolution.
              
(5) Changed:   Use realignment in "cat_tst_calc_kappa" in case of different 
               resolution only if realign parameter is true. Otherwise, imcalc
               is used directly.
(6) Changed:   Updated help texts in cat_conf_opts and reduce the amount of 
               control parameters. 
(7) Changed:   Added resolution dependency in cat_vol_sanlm to reduce the amout
               of filtering in low resolution data. 


== Bug fixes ==
(1) Fixed:     Corrected bugs in cat_run_APP_init.
(2) Fixed:     Corrected Ym intensity scaling problem in cat_main_LAS.
(3) Fixed:     Corrected index error in cat_surf_smooth.
               Thanks to Björn Horing for pointing out this bug.
(4) Fixed:     Corrected WMH volume output in CAT report and XML file.
               Thanks to M.H.T. Zwartbol for pointing out this bug.
(5) Fixed:     Corrected simultan output of modulated data in expert mode in 
               cat_io_writenii and cat_main.
               Thanks to Felix Hoffstaedter for pointing out this limitation.
(6) Fixed:     Corrected typo in SPM PBT figure.
(7) Fixed:     Special case in PBT data processing of binary data.

M       cat_io_writenii.m
M       cat_run_job.m
M       cat_surf_createCS.m
M       cat_tst_cattest.m
M       cat_vol_pbt.m

(1) Changed: Removed tca and replaced this approach by a local change of 
    intensities for creating the initial surface. In the parahippocampal 
    area the intensity of the ppi image is inceased. This prevents large 
    cuts in that area. In the cortex the ppi intensity is decreased which
    helps in preventing glued gyri/sulci.
(2) Changed: Added two new parameters to control surface creation in 
    cortex and parahippocampal gyrus.
(3) Changed: Typos...

M       templates_animals/monkey_oldworld_Template_6.nii
M       templates_animals/monkey_oldworld_brainmask.nii
M       templates_animals/monkey_oldworld_vbm12.nii

(1) Changed:    Separate the bias, noise and intensity corrected image (Ym)  
                into two subversion with global (Ym) and local (Ymi) intensity 
                normalization. The Ym is more reasonable for myelination 
                analysis, whereas the Ymi more sensible for the tissue classes.
                Also for Ym LAS is used to correct reminding WM inhomogeneities.
                The output of the local normalized image is only assessable via
                cat_defaults (cat.output.las) and expert GUI.
                The CAT ROIs will extract the intensities of the Ym rather of 
                the Ymi. The CAT report now shows the Ym rather than the Ymi.
(2) Changed:    Added ROI menu to expert GUI.
(3) Fixed:      Volume creation error in TCA part of cat_surf_createCS.
(4) Fixed:      Update version of cat_surf_render.
(5) Changed:    Added surface type check in cat_surf_resamp to ignore
                '.central.' and '.sphere.'.                
(6) Fixed:      Fast correction of side flip in animal atlas maps.

    correction and will check whether the Hausdorff distance in the 
    parahippocampal gyrus will be too large. In that case a new run with
    BrainSuite topology correction (tca) is made to prevent large cuts in that 
    gyrus.

    Haussdorff distance multiplied with mean curvature to decide whether
    the defect is a hole or handle.

          and the expected results exist.

          preprocessing of some subjects or complete jobs failed by internal 
          (small cat errors) or external (matlab or systems error, server errors).

r808 | dahnke | 2015-12-03 10:19:36 +0100 (Do, 03 Dez 2015) | 31 lines

Changed paths:
M       CHANGES.txt
M       cat_main.m
M       cat_run.m
M       cat_surf_createCS.m
M       cat_surf_display.m
M       cat_surf_vol2surf.m
A       internal/cat_vol_atlas.m
 M      templates_1.50mm

New:     Added internal cat_vol_atlas function to normalize, optimize and merge
         common atlas datasets such as AAL, IBSR, HAMMERS, ANATOMY, MORI, LPBA40,
         Neuromorphometrics,  ... 
         The function optimize, normalize and merge the atlas ROIs of one or 
         multiple subjects as 4D probability map to create a single 3D atlas map. 
         It use CAT preprocessing and median filtering to optimize and normalize
         the individual atlas ROIs and try to rename the ROI names given by the 
         CSV Files by a dictionary. 
         The function is still in development, the principle idea works, but 
         the naming is not correct for all regions. 
Changed: Replace SPM PS by MATLAB print function to write CAT report as PDF, 
         because the PS is outdated and does not work with surfaces.  
Changed: Common print structure in cat_surf_display and cat_main.
Changed: Added SPM command line link for cat_surf_vol2surf output, if job.verb 
         is >0.  
Fixed:   Corrected surface colormap and scaling after changing to SPM gray.
Fixed:   Double surface output in CAT report.
Fixed:   Changed thickness field estimation and fixed writing in XML file. 
Comment: Added ;; in MATLAB code to mark special lines to jump in the editor.

     with APP parameter in cg_vbm_defaults and experimental expert GUI option. 
     APP include a bias rough bias correction and brain extraction to support 
     untypical cases (non-human/neonates) with registration problems.

     low GM intensities were not corrected and therefore misclassified as CSF.
     Further tiny changes to stabilize the CSF/background field.
